Initialzes F\+C\+C\+OB registers for Program check command. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Peripheral\+Base} & Pointer to a peripheral registers structure (peripheral base address). You can use the constant defined in the registers definition header file ($<$peripheral$>$\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+TR) or the constant defined in the peripheral initialization component header file ($<$component\+\_\+name$>$\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+CE). \\
\hline
{\em Address} & Flash address in the flash block. Must be longword aligned. This parameter is a 24-\/bit value. \\
\hline
{\em Data} & Expected data. This parameter is a 32-\/bit value. \\
\hline
{\em Margin\+Level} & Read-\/1 margin choice. Use constants from group \char`\"{}\+Margin
       level constants\char`\"{}. This parameter is 8 bits wide. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Initialzes F\+C\+C\+OB registers for Program longword command. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Peripheral\+Base} & Pointer to a peripheral registers structure (peripheral base address). You can use the constant defined in the registers definition header file ($<$peripheral$>$\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+TR) or the constant defined in the peripheral initialization component header file ($<$component\+\_\+name$>$\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+CE). \\
\hline
{\em Address} & Flash address in the flash block. Must be 32-\/bit aligned. This parameter is a 24-\/bit value. \\
\hline
{\em Data} & Longword to be written. This parameter is a 32-\/bit value. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Initialzes F\+C\+C\+OB registers for Read 1s section command. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Peripheral\+Base} & Pointer to a peripheral registers structure (peripheral base address). You can use the constant defined in the registers definition header file ($<$peripheral$>$\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+TR) or the constant defined in the peripheral initialization component header file ($<$component\+\_\+name$>$\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+CE). \\
\hline
{\em Address} & Flash address in the flash block to be verified. This parameter is a 24-\/bit value. \\
\hline
{\em Section\+Unit\+Count} & Number of section units to be verified. This parameter is a 16-\/bit value. \\
\hline
{\em Margin\+Level} & Read-\/1 margin choice. Use constants from group \char`\"{}\+Margin
       level constants\char`\"{}. This parameter is 8 bits wide. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns a value of void type.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define F\+T\+F\+A\+\_\+\+P\+D\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+F\+C\+C\+O\+B\+Address(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{Peripheral\+Base,  }\item[{}]{Address }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
( \(\backslash\)
    (\hyperlink{group___f_t_f_a___register___accessor___macros_gae685c7a7a80187d3c2d6f5404e5e3ebd}{FTFA\_FCCOB3\_REG}(PeripheralBase) = \(\backslash\)
     (uint8\_t)(Address)), \(\backslash\)
    ((\hyperlink{group___f_t_f_a___register___accessor___macros_gafb84447c23c2c9ee77f894f846161b5d}{FTFA\_FCCOB2\_REG}(PeripheralBase) = \(\backslash\)
     (uint8\_t)((uint32\_t)(Address) >> 8U)), \(\backslash\)
    (\hyperlink{group___f_t_f_a___register___accessor___macros_gab2a718345513411b315eee6a7cfdb08a}{FTFA\_FCCOB1\_REG}(PeripheralBase) = \(\backslash\)
     (uint8\_t)((uint32\_t)(Address) >> 16U))) \(\backslash\)
  )
\end{DoxyCode}


Writes the value to the F\+C\+C\+OB Address register. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Peripheral\+Base} & Pointer to a peripheral registers structure (peripheral base address). You can use the constant defined in the registers definition header file ($<$peripheral$>$\+\_\+\+B\+A\+S\+E\+\_\+\+P\+TR) or the constant defined in the peripheral initialization component header file ($<$component\+\_\+name$>$\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+CE). \\
\hline
{\em Address} & Value written to the F\+C\+C\+OB Address register. This parameter is a 24-\/bit value. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Returns a value of void type. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The macro accesses the following registers\+: F\+T\+F\+A\+\_\+\+F\+C\+C\+O\+B3, F\+T\+F\+A\+\_\+\+F\+C\+C\+O\+B2, F\+T\+F\+A\+\_\+\+F\+C\+C\+O\+B1 (depending on the peripheral). 
\end{DoxyRemark}
